Producer documentation / Standard MIDI idea generator

jamburgr

Generate MIDI ideas, drag them into your DAW, choose sounds you love, and iterate. jamburgr is a MIDI-only Python instrument for chord, bass, pad, lead, optional drum, compact arrangement, and full-song producer sketches shaped by styles, Roman numerals, voicings, and rhythmic patterns.

Generate your first pack Choose a style
script jamburgr.py
format Standard MIDI
runtime Python stdlib
first command
python jamburgr.py --config jamburgr_example_recipe.md --explain-only
Quick operating loop

From a musical direction to a DAW-ready MIDI pack.

Pick a key and style, generate a pack, then audition the MIDI on your own instruments. jamburgr does not generate audio; its optional drum/percussion lanes are editable General MIDI notes for your own kits, racks, samplers, or hardware.

01ConfigKey, scale, style, progression
02HarmonyRoman numerals to chord roots
03VoicingClosed, wide, drop2, voice-led
04PatternPulses, stabs, gates, arps
05LayersChord, bass, pad, lead, and optional drums
06SectionsCompact sketches or full-song forms

Interactive

terminal
python jamburgr.py

Pack

terminal
python jamburgr.py --key "F# minor" --chord minor_add9 --style future_bass --output-mode pack

Config file

terminal
python jamburgr.py --config my_song.md
Current scope

Built for fast, chord-first electronic music sketching with enough structure to keep ideas moving.

Use jamburgr when you want a harmonic seed, a layer stack, a drum scaffold, or a sectioned MIDI sketch. Bring your own samples, synth patches, drum sounds, and taste; the generated files are meant to be edited, arranged, and made yours.

HarmonyMajor, minor, sevenths, ninths, sus, quartal, clusters
ScalesMajor, minor modes, pentatonics, blues minor, chromatic
VoicingOpen, wide, drop2, inversions, rootless, shell, auto voice-leading
PatternsGates, pulses, stabs, Euclidean rhythms, seeded arpeggios
BassRoot notes, house offbeats, techno rolls, 303 accents, 808 subs
PadsSustained chords, wide beds, high shimmer, drones, smooth top notes
LeadsSeeded motifs, chord-tone hooks, pentatonic lines, plucks, arps
DrumsOptional GM drum lanes, style presets, density, and swing hints
PresetsStyle-aware scale hints, registers, layer modes, and lead feel
VariationsSeeded v01/v02/v03 takes without changing key or progression
ExplainResolved roots, chord names, notes, layer choices, and planned outputs
ArrangementSequential compact sections or style-aware full-song producer sketches
Exportsingle, multi, both, pack, full arrangement lanes, and section MIDI files
WorkflowCLI flags, interactive prompts, DEFAULT_CONFIG, Markdown configs
BoundariesMIDI-only; no audio rendering, samples, or song duplication
The Jam Library

Style-aware defaults with producer context.

The atlas turns jamburgr's style presets into a learning surface: each style shows tempo, scale, groove feel, harmonic habits, layer roles, drum preset/density/swing, General MIDI routing guidance, reference canon context, producer exercises, and source IDs.

Style details

Reference canon, sound-design vocabulary, and DAW exercises.

bass music / 150 BPM / future_bass

Future bass / wonky emotional

Future bass grew from post-dubstep, trap, wonky, and internet beat scenes into a chord-forward festival and streaming-era language.

AKA
future bass, wonky bass, melodic trap-adjacent bass
Geography
UK and North American bass scenes, online producer communities, and festival bass stages.
Era
2010s-present
Groove feel
Half-time or syncopated drums with strong downbeat weight, spacious snare placement, and sub-focused movement.
Harmonic habits
Minor-mode loops, suspended color tones, add9 sonorities, and dramatic tension between bass roots and bright upper stacks.

Layer defaults

Scale
natural_minor
Voicing
wide
Pattern
syncopated_pads
Bass
root_fifth_octave @ octave 1
Pad
high_shimmer @ octave 5
Lead
future_bass_chop @ octave 5
Lead feel
medium / medium
Drum style
half_time
Drum density
medium
Drum swing
0%

Drum role

Half-time — Wide snare spacing and downbeat weight for bass music, dubstep, and wave/hardwave.

Choose a heavy kit or sampler lane, then tune kick/snare length around the bass line.

Density medium. Sparse leaves lots of room; medium adds hats; dense adds extra top movement and impact. Swing hint: 0%. Drum export is General MIDI only; enable it with generate_drums: true.

Producer setup recipe

Use this as a practical Ableton-friendly starting point, then choose your own sounds and edit the MIDI for the track you are making.

Chords
Ableton Wavetable or Analog for poly chords, with a hardware-friendly subtractive poly patch as an alternative
Bass
Ableton Drift, Analog, or Operator for a clean mono bass that follows the generated root motion
Pad
Ableton Wavetable, Meld, or Analog for a sustained pad layer that can be muted or widened independently
Lead
Ableton Wavetable/Drift short pluck or chopped sampler layer with MIDI kept original and editable
Drums
Use the generated General MIDI drum lane with an Ableton Drum Rack, GM kit, or hardware drum route. Start from `half_time` at `medium` density with 0% swing, then swap kit pieces and edit accents in the piano roll.
Routing
Keep bass, drums, chords, pads, and lead on separate MIDI tracks. Center the sub layer, leave headroom for kick/snare weight, and use sidechain or volume shaping only after the MIDI idea is working.
Effects
Ableton stock starting chain: EQ Eight cleanup, Saturator for controlled edge, Compressor or sidechain ducking, and Echo/Reverb sends for impacts.
Ableton bridge setup
Ableton bridge-ready direction: keep each generated layer on its own track, use stock devices or personal racks, and save any favorite setup as a jamburgr rack with stable macros.
Listen for
Listen for the relationship between sub movement, snare placement, wide harmony, and moments where the arrangement gets smaller before it gets larger. Also compare the generated groove feel against: Half-time or syncopated drums with strong downbeat weight, spacious snare placement, and sub-focused movement.
Chords

polyphonic chord synth

Clear harmonic color that supports the groove without covering bass, lead, or drums.

Mix role
Midrange harmonic identity; high-pass and balance below the lead but above bass fundamentals.
Effects/routing
Start with EQ cleanup, filter movement, and shared delay/reverb sends rather than printing effects into the MIDI idea.
Hardware
Prophet-10-style poly patches are a strong hardware option for warm chords, stabs, and pads.
Tags
stock_ableton, saved_rack_ready, hardware_poly, commercial_core_synth_optional
Bass

clean mono bass synth

Centered low-end motion that makes the generated roots feel intentional and editable.

Mix role
Centered low-end anchor; keep it mono-friendly and leave headroom for drums.
Effects/routing
Use EQ and light saturation; avoid wide modulation below the sub range and add sidechain or volume shaping only after the groove works.
Hardware
Moog Matriarch-style mono patches work well for bass, acid-style lines, resonant plucks, and hardware takes.
Tags
stock_ableton, saved_rack_ready, hardware_mono
Pad

wide sustained pad synth

High, bright support that can be softened with filter and reverb if it competes with the lead.

Mix role
Background width and emotional scale; keep it quieter than chords and automate section entrances.
Effects/routing
Use chorus, width, reverb, or slow filter movement on sends so the pad can be muted or thinned quickly.
Hardware
Prophet-10-style poly patches are a strong hardware option for warm chords, stabs, and pads.
Tags
stock_ableton, saved_rack_ready, hardware_poly, commercial_core_synth_optional
Lead

short pluck or chopped sampler layer

Editable top-line idea that should guide the sketch, not become a finished melody by default.

Mix role
Foreground hook or response layer; make it audible without masking chord attacks.
Effects/routing
Use tempo delay or short reverb sends; keep the dry note shape readable for editing.
Hardware
Moog Matriarch-style mono patches work well for bass, acid-style lines, resonant plucks, and hardware takes.
Tags
stock_ableton, saved_rack_ready, hardware_mono, commercial_core_synth_optional
Drums

General MIDI drum instrument or Drum Rack

half time drum scaffold at medium density with 0% swing for DAW editing.

Mix role
Transient and groove reference; route to an editable drum instrument and balance before adding heavy processing.
Effects/routing
Use Drum Rack or a GM-compatible kit first, then swap sounds, tune hits, and add Drum Buss or saturation to taste.
Hardware
External drum machines or sampler kits can follow the General MIDI lane after note mapping is checked.
Tags
stock_ableton, saved_rack_ready, general_midi, drum_rack
sub basssupersaw stacksvocal chopspitched percussionwide synth chords

Gear and synthesis

DAW samplers, wavetable synths, Roland TR-808 lineage, sidechain compressors

detuned saw layers, pitch envelopes, formant or vocal resampling, sub layering, wide unison modulation

Listen for

intro atmosphere, pre-drop reduction, impact-led drops, call-and-response chord hooks

sidechain ducking, bright reverb throws, parallel saturation, wide stereo chorusing

Try this in your DAW

  • Write an original four-bar minor loop, then reharmonize the top voices while keeping the bass roots stable.
  • Design one soft chord layer and one bright layer, then automate their balance across an eight-bar phrase.
  • Export separate chord, bass, pad, lead, and optional drum MIDI lanes so the DAW session stays easy to arrange.

bass music / 145 BPM / melodic_bass

Melodic bass / anthem drop

Melodic bass connects dubstep's half-time weight with trance-sized harmony, pop toplines, and cinematic breakdowns.

AKA
melodic bass, melodic dubstep, anthemic bass
Geography
UK and North American bass scenes, online producer communities, and festival bass stages.
Era
2010s-present
Groove feel
Half-time or syncopated drums with strong downbeat weight, spacious snare placement, and sub-focused movement.
Harmonic habits
Minor-mode loops, suspended color tones, add9 sonorities, and dramatic tension between bass roots and bright upper stacks.

Voicing

Drum density

Drum swing

Drum role

Half-time — Wide snare spacing and downbeat weight for bass music, dubstep, and wave/hardwave.

Choose a heavy kit or sampler lane, then tune kick/snare length around the bass line.

Density medium. Sparse leaves lots of room; medium adds hats; dense adds extra top movement and impact. Swing hint: 0%. Drum export is General MIDI only; enable it with generate_drums: true.

Producer setup recipe

Use this as a practical Ableton-friendly starting point, then choose your own sounds and edit the MIDI for the track you are making.

Chords
Ableton Wavetable or Analog for poly chords, with a hardware-friendly subtractive poly patch as an alternative
Bass

Pad
Ableton Wavetable, Meld, or Analog for a sustained pad layer that can be muted or widened independently
Lead
Ableton Operator, Drift, or Wavetable for a simple motif or chord-tone lead above the harmony
Drums
Use the generated General MIDI drum lane with an Ableton Drum Rack, GM kit, or hardware drum route. Start from `half_time` at `medium` density with 0% swing, then swap kit pieces and edit accents in the piano roll.
Routing
Keep bass, drums, chords, pads, and lead on separate MIDI tracks. Center the sub layer, leave headroom for kick/snare weight, and use sidechain or volume shaping only after the MIDI idea is working.
Effects
Ableton stock starting chain: EQ Eight cleanup, Saturator for controlled edge, Compressor or sidechain ducking, and Echo/Reverb sends for impacts.
Ableton bridge setup
Ableton bridge-ready direction: keep each generated layer on its own track, use stock devices or personal racks, and save any favorite setup as a jamburgr rack with stable macros.
Listen for
Listen for the relationship between sub movement, snare placement, wide harmony, and moments where the arrangement gets smaller before it gets larger. Also compare the generated groove feel against: Half-time or syncopated drums with strong downbeat weight, spacious snare placement, and sub-focused movement.
Chords

polyphonic chord synth

Clear harmonic color that supports the groove without covering bass, lead, or drums.

Mix role
Midrange harmonic identity; high-pass and balance below the lead but above bass fundamentals.
Effects/routing
Start with EQ cleanup, filter movement, and shared delay/reverb sends rather than printing effects into the MIDI idea.
Hardware
Prophet-10-style poly patches are a strong hardware option for warm chords, stabs, and pads.
Tags
stock_ableton, saved_rack_ready, hardware_poly, commercial_core_synth_optional

Drum role

Ambient sparse — Minimal percussive markers for chill, ambient techno, downtempo, and hazy pop lanes.

Route to soft percussion, foley, or a muted kit and keep velocities low.

Density sparse. Sparse is nearly empty; medium adds small markers; dense adds a quiet shaker bed. Swing hint: 12%. Drum export is General MIDI only; enable it with generate_drums: true.

Producer setup recipe

Use this as a practical Ableton-friendly starting point, then choose your own sounds and edit the MIDI for the track you are making.

Chords
Ableton Wavetable/Analog for warm wide chords, or Prophet-10-style pads with slow filter movement
Bass
Ableton Drift, Analog, or Operator for a clean mono bass that follows the generated root motion
Pad
Ableton Wavetable or Prophet-10-style slow pad with chorus, long release, and gentle high-end rolloff
Lead
Ableton Operator, Drift, or Wavetable for a simple motif or chord-tone lead above the harmony
Drums
Use the generated General MIDI drum lane with an Ableton Drum Rack, GM kit, or hardware drum route. Start from `ambient_sparse` at `sparse` density with 12% swing, then swap kit pieces and edit accents in the piano roll.
Routing
Use wide pads/chords, a centered bass track, and a soft drum or percussion lane. Keep delay/reverb on returns so the sketch stays easy to rebalance.
Effects
Ableton stock starting chain: Chorus-Ensemble or subtle modulation, EQ Eight, Echo, Hybrid Reverb/Reverb sends, and gentle bus compression.
Ableton bridge setup
Ableton bridge-ready direction: start with stock synth or rack choices, then map stable macros such as Tone, Movement, Brightness, Drive, Width, FX, Attack, and Release for fast style-aware setup.
Listen for
Listen for pad width, simple bass movement, nostalgic timbre, and the way reverb/delay length changes emotional scale. Also compare the generated groove feel against: Relaxed tempos, steady arps, soft syncopation, and nostalgia-forward chord sustain.

Progressive house

Progressive house developed through club culture, then became a major festival language through melodic breakdowns and large drops.

AKA
progressive house, festival progressive, melodic house anthem
Geography
Chicago, New York, London, Paris, Ibiza, South Africa, and global club circuits.
Era
1990s-present
Groove feel
Four-on-the-floor pulse with swung percussion, offbeat emphasis, and loop-friendly chord movement.

Short modal cells, seventh chords, add9 colors, and progressions that leave room for drums and bass.

Producer setup recipe

Use this as a practical Ableton-friendly starting point, then choose your own sounds and edit the MIDI for the track you are making.

Chords
Ableton Analog/Drift for short filtered stabs, or Prophet-10-style poly stabs with a fast amp envelope
Bass
Ableton Drift or Analog mono bass with short decay, centered low end, and enough filter movement to answer the kick
Pad
Ableton Wavetable, Meld, or Analog for a sustained pad layer that can be muted or widened independently
Lead
Ableton Operator, Drift, or Wavetable for a simple motif or chord-tone lead above the harmony
Drums
Use the generated General MIDI drum lane with an Ableton Drum Rack, GM kit, or hardware drum route. Start from `four_on_floor` at `medium` density with 0% swing, then swap kit pieces and edit accents in the piano roll.
Routing
Route drums to a General MIDI Drum Rack or kit, keep bass mono and separate from chord stabs, and use returns for delay/reverb so loop edits stay fast.
Effects
Ableton stock starting chain: EQ Eight high-pass on chords, Auto Filter for movement, Glue Compressor on the music bus, and short Delay/Reverb sends.
Ableton bridge setup
Ableton bridge-ready direction: start with stock synth or rack choices, then map stable macros such as Tone, Movement, Brightness, Drive, Width, FX, Attack, and Release for fast style-aware setup.
Listen for
Listen for how short chord stabs, offbeat bass, swung percussion, and small mutes make a loop feel alive without constant new material. Also compare the generated groove feel against: Four-on-the-floor pulse with swung percussion, offbeat emphasis, and loop-friendly chord movement.

Listen for how short chord stabs, offbeat bass, swung percussion, and small mutes make a loop feel alive without constant new material. Also compare the generated groove feel against: Four-on-the-floor pulse with swung percussion, offbeat emphasis, and loop-friendly chord movement.
Chords

short filtered chord stab instrument

Clear harmonic color that supports the groove without covering bass, lead, or drums.

Mix role
Midrange harmonic identity; high-pass and balance below the lead but above bass fundamentals.
Effects/routing
Start with EQ cleanup, filter movement, and shared delay/reverb sends rather than printing effects into the MIDI idea.
Hardware
Prophet-10-style poly patches are a strong hardware option for warm chords, stabs, and pads.

clean mono bass synth

Centered low-end motion that makes the generated roots feel intentional and editable.

Mix role
Centered low-end anchor; keep it mono-friendly and leave headroom for drums.
Effects/routing

Try this in your DAW

Era

Drum style
four_on_floor
Drum density
dense
Drum swing
0%

Drum role

Four-on-the-floor — Steady kick pulse for house, trance, synthwave, and other grid-forward ideas.

Drop the lane onto a General MIDI kit or Drum Rack, then choose a kick, clap, and hat palette that fits the track.

Density dense. Sparse keeps kick/clap shape; medium adds offbeat hats; dense adds busier hats and lift. Swing hint: 0%. Drum export is General MIDI only; enable it with generate_drums: true.

Producer setup recipe

Use this as a practical Ableton-friendly starting point, then choose your own sounds and edit the MIDI for the track you are making.

Chords
Ableton Wavetable/Analog for gated chords or rave stabs, with a hardware poly option for wide sustained layers
Bass
Ableton Drift, Analog, or Operator for a clean mono bass that follows the generated root motion
Pad
Ableton Wavetable, Meld, or Analog for a sustained pad layer that can be muted or widened independently
Lead
Ableton Operator or Wavetable pluck with tempo delay, or a Matriarch-style resonant mono pluck for hardware takes
Drums
Use the generated General MIDI drum lane with an Ableton Drum Rack, GM kit, or hardware drum route. Start from `four_on_floor` at `dense` density with 0% swing, then swap kit pieces and edit accents in the piano roll.
Routing
Use separate tracks for pulse, drones, arps, and drums. Keep the kick/bass lane focused, then automate filters or mutes across sections instead of overfilling the MIDI.
Effects
Ableton stock starting chain: Auto Filter automation, Saturator or Roar for drive if available, Echo on arps, and large reverb sends for breakdown space.
Ableton bridge setup
Ableton bridge-ready direction: start with stock synth or rack choices, then map stable macros such as Tone, Movement, Brightness, Drive, Width, FX, Attack, and Release for fast style-aware setup.
Listen for
Listen for gradual filter motion, pedal tones, gated or arpeggiated repetition, and long tension curves across sections. Also compare the generated groove feel against: Motorik repetition, steady kick pressure, gated arps, and hypnotic phrase evolution.

Centered low-end motion that makes the generated roots feel intentional and editable.

Mix role
Centered low-end anchor; keep it mono-friendly and leave headroom for drums.
Effects/routing
Use EQ and light saturation; avoid wide modulation below the sub range and add sidechain or volume shaping only after the groove works.
Hardware
Moog Matriarch-style mono patches work well for bass, acid-style lines, resonant plucks, and hardware takes.
Tags
stock_ableton, saved_rack_ready, hardware_mono
Pad

drone or sustained atmosphere instrument

Slow, steady harmonic bed that adds scale context without stealing rhythmic focus.

Mix role
Background width and emotional scale; keep it quieter than chords and automate section entrances.
Effects/routing
Use chorus, width, reverb, or slow filter movement on sends so the pad can be muted or thinned quickly.
Hardware
Prophet-10-style poly patches are a strong hardware option for warm chords, stabs, and pads.
Tags
stock_ableton, saved_rack_ready, hardware_poly, commercial_core_synth_optional
Lead

pluck or arpeggiated lead synth

Bright, tempo-aware pluck motion that can be automated or muted across sections.

Mix role
Foreground hook or response layer; make it audible without masking chord attacks.
Effects/routing
Use tempo delay or short reverb sends; keep the dry note shape readable for editing.
Hardware
Moog Matriarch-style mono patches work well for bass, acid-style lines, resonant plucks, and hardware takes.
Tags
stock_ableton, saved_rack_ready, hardware_mono, commercial_core_synth_optional
Drums

General MIDI drum instrument or Drum Rack

techno drive drum scaffold at dense density with 0% swing for DAW editing.

Mix role
Transient and groove reference; route to an editable drum instrument and balance before adding heavy processing.
Effects/routing
Use Drum Rack or a GM-compatible kit first, then swap sounds, tune hits, and add Drum Buss or saturation to taste.
Hardware
External drum machines or sampler kits can follow the General MIDI lane after note mapping is checked.
Tags
stock_ableton, saved_rack_ready, general_midi, drum_rack
analog-style bassgated supersawsFM bellsrave stabssequenced arps

Gear and synthesis

Roland TR-909 lineage, Roland TB-303 lineage, step sequencers, analog monosynths

resonant filter sweeps, tempo-synced gates, acid slides, supersaw detune, FM plucks

Listen for

long builds, filter-open tension, drum-led breakdowns, return-to-groove drops

tempo delay, large hall reverb, drive saturation, sidechain compression

Try this in your DAW

  • Limit the harmony to one or two Roman numerals and make motion through inversion, register, and pattern.
  • Render a pack, then mute lanes one by one to find the smallest loop that still carries the style.
  • Write a sixteen-bar section where the chord MIDI stays stable but lead density rises gradually.

Reference canon artists

  1. Charlotte de Witte
  2. Amelie Lens
  3. Adam Beyer
  4. Carl Cox
  5. Jeff Mills
  6. Surgeon
  7. Ben Klock
  8. Dax J
  9. ANNA
  10. I Hate Models

Reference canon tracks

  1. Charlotte de Witte - Selected (2015)
  2. Amelie Lens - Exhale (2017)
  3. Adam Beyer - Your Mind (2018)
  4. Carl Cox - Phuture 2000 (1999)
  5. Jeff Mills - The Bells (1996)
  6. Surgeon - La Real (1996)
  7. Ben Klock - Subzero (2009)
  8. Dax J - Escape the System (2015)
  9. ANNA - Hidden Beauties (2018)
  10. I Hate Models - Daydream (2016)

techno and trance / 112 BPM / ambient_techno

Ambient techno

Ambient techno merges techno's pulse with ambient listening-space design and dub-influenced depth.

AKA
ambient techno, deep techno, atmospheric techno
Geography
Detroit, Berlin, Frankfurt, Goa, the Netherlands, and international warehouse/festival scenes.
Era
1990s-present
Groove feel
Motorik repetition, steady kick pressure, gated arps, and hypnotic phrase evolution.
Harmonic habits
Modal minor movement, pedal tones, chromatic tension, and long arcs built from small cells.

Layer defaults

Scale
natural_minor
Voicing
open
Pattern
cinematic_swells
Bass
pedal_tone @ octave 1
Pad
evolving_inversions @ octave 4
Lead
melodic_techno_pluck @ octave 5
Lead feel
sparse / high
Drum style
ambient_sparse
Drum density
sparse
Drum swing
8%

Drum role

Ambient sparse — Minimal percussive markers for chill, ambient techno, downtempo, and hazy pop lanes.

Route to soft percussion, foley, or a muted kit and keep velocities low.

Density sparse. Sparse is nearly empty; medium adds small markers; dense adds a quiet shaker bed. Swing hint: 8%. Drum export is General MIDI only; enable it with generate_drums: true.

Producer setup recipe

Use this as a practical Ableton-friendly starting point, then choose your own sounds and edit the MIDI for the track you are making.

Chords
Ableton Wavetable/Analog for gated chords or rave stabs, with a hardware poly option for wide sustained layers
Bass
Ableton Drift, Analog, or Operator for a clean mono bass that follows the generated root motion
Pad
Ableton Wavetable, Meld, or Analog for a sustained pad layer that can be muted or widened independently
Lead
Ableton Operator or Wavetable pluck with tempo delay, or a Matriarch-style resonant mono pluck for hardware takes
Drums
Use the generated General MIDI drum lane with an Ableton Drum Rack, GM kit, or hardware drum route. Start from `ambient_sparse` at `sparse` density with 8% swing, then swap kit pieces and edit accents in the piano roll.
Routing
Use separate tracks for pulse, drones, arps, and drums. Keep the kick/bass lane focused, then automate filters or mutes across sections instead of overfilling the MIDI.
Effects
Ableton stock starting chain: Auto Filter automation, Saturator or Roar for drive if available, Echo on arps, and large reverb sends for breakdown space.
Ableton bridge setup
Ableton bridge profile: stock-device setup with layer-specific volume balance and simple tone controls. Use saved jamburgr racks later if you want a more personal sound while keeping the same MIDI.
Listen for
Listen for gradual filter motion, pedal tones, gated or arpeggiated repetition, and long tension curves across sections. Also compare the generated groove feel against: Motorik repetition, steady kick pressure, gated arps, and hypnotic phrase evolution.
Chords

polyphonic chord synth

Clear harmonic color that supports the groove without covering bass, lead, or drums.

Mix role
Midrange harmonic identity; high-pass and balance below the lead but above bass fundamentals.
Effects/routing
Start with EQ cleanup, filter movement, and shared delay/reverb sends rather than printing effects into the MIDI idea.
Hardware
Prophet-10-style poly patches are a strong hardware option for warm chords, stabs, and pads.
Tags
stock_ableton, saved_rack_ready, hardware_poly, commercial_core_synth_optional

house / 124 BPM / acid_house

Acid house / 303 companion chords

Acid house formed around experiments with the Roland TB-303 and became central to late-1980s club and rave culture.

AKA
acid house, 303 house, acid
Geography
Chicago, New York, London, Paris, Ibiza, South Africa, and global club circuits.
Era
1980s-present
Groove feel
Four-on-the-floor pulse with swung percussion, offbeat emphasis, and loop-friendly chord movement.
Harmonic habits
Short modal cells, seventh chords, add9 colors, and progressions that leave room for drums and bass.

Layer defaults

Scale
natural_minor
Voicing
closed
Pattern
offbeat_stabs
Bass
acid_303 @ octave 2
Pad
fifth_drone @ octave 4
Lead
simple_motif @ octave 5
Lead feel
sparse / high
Drum style
four_on_floor
Drum density
medium
Drum swing
0%

Drum role

Four-on-the-floor — Steady kick pulse for house, trance, synthwave, and other grid-forward ideas.

Drop the lane onto a General MIDI kit or Drum Rack, then choose a kick, clap, and hat palette that fits the track.

Density medium. Sparse keeps kick/clap shape; medium adds offbeat hats; dense adds busier hats and lift. Swing hint: 0%. Drum export is General MIDI only; enable it with generate_drums: true.

Producer setup recipe

Use this as a practical Ableton-friendly starting point, then choose your own sounds and edit the MIDI for the track you are making.

Chords
Ableton Analog/Drift for short filtered stabs, or Prophet-10-style poly stabs with a fast amp envelope
Bass
Ableton Drift resonant mono bass, or a Matriarch-style single-oscillator line with envelope-driven filter resonance
Pad
Ableton Wavetable or Analog drone with slow attack, low resonance, and subtle movement
Lead
Ableton Operator, Drift, or Wavetable for a simple motif or chord-tone lead above the harmony
Drums
Use the generated General MIDI drum lane with an Ableton Drum Rack, GM kit, or hardware drum route. Start from `four_on_floor` at `medium` density with 0% swing, then swap kit pieces and edit accents in the piano roll.
Routing
Route drums to a General MIDI Drum Rack or kit, keep bass mono and separate from chord stabs, and use returns for delay/reverb so loop edits stay fast.
Effects
Ableton stock starting chain: EQ Eight high-pass on chords, Auto Filter for movement, Glue Compressor on the music bus, and short Delay/Reverb sends.
Ableton bridge setup
Ableton bridge profile: stock-device setup with layer-specific volume balance and simple tone controls. Use saved jamburgr racks later if you want a more personal sound while keeping the same MIDI.
Listen for
Listen for how short chord stabs, offbeat bass, swung percussion, and small mutes make a loop feel alive without constant new material. Also compare the generated groove feel against: Four-on-the-floor pulse with swung percussion, offbeat emphasis, and loop-friendly chord movement.

electric pianoorgan stabssampled chord chopssub bassdrum machine percussion

Gear and synthesis

Roland TR-909 lineage, Roland TR-808 lineage, Akai-style samplers, MIDI chord modules

filter envelopes, sample filtering, short amp envelopes, chorused keys, subtractive bass patches

Listen for

DJ-friendly intros, incremental mutes, breakdowns, drop returns, loop variation

bus compression, delay sends, filtered transitions, spring or plate reverb

Try this in your DAW

  • Make a two-chord groove and change only rhythm, voicing, and bass placement over sixteen bars.
  • Create an original offbeat chord stab layer, then duplicate it an octave up for a lighter variation.
  • Use pack mode to compare chord, bass, and pad lanes as separate DAW clips.

house / 122 BPM / deep_house

Deep house

Deep house emerged by blending Chicago house with soul, jazz-funk, and smoother chord language.

AKA
deep house, soulful house, jazzy house
Geography
Chicago, New York, London, Paris, Ibiza, South Africa, and global club circuits.
Era
1980s-present
Groove feel
Four-on-the-floor pulse with swung percussion, offbeat emphasis, and loop-friendly chord movement.
Harmonic habits
Short modal cells, seventh chords, add9 colors, and progressions that leave room for drums and bass.

Layer defaults

Scale
natural_minor
Voicing
drop2
Pattern
offbeat_stabs
Bass
offbeat_house @ octave 1
Pad
slow_wide @ octave 4
Lead
chord_tone_lead @ octave 5
Lead feel
sparse / medium
Drum style
house_shuffle
Drum density
medium
Drum swing
18%

Drum role

House shuffle — A swung club scaffold with kick/clap weight and loose hat or shaker motion.

Use a warm Drum Rack, 909-style kit, or sampled house kit and keep the hats editable for groove feel.

Density medium. Sparse sketches the pocket; medium adds shuffled hats; dense adds extra top-loop energy. Swing hint: 18%. Drum export is General MIDI only; enable it with generate_drums: true.

Producer setup recipe

Use this as a practical Ableton-friendly starting point, then choose your own sounds and edit the MIDI for the track you are making.

Chords
Ableton Analog/Drift for short filtered stabs, or Prophet-10-style poly stabs with a fast amp envelope
Bass
Ableton Drift or Analog mono bass with short decay, centered low end, and enough filter movement to answer the kick
Pad
Ableton Wavetable, Meld, or Analog for a sustained pad layer that can be muted or widened independently
Lead
Ableton Operator, Drift, or Wavetable for a simple motif or chord-tone lead above the harmony
Drums
Use the generated General MIDI drum lane with an Ableton Drum Rack, GM kit, or hardware drum route. Start from `house_shuffle` at `medium` density with 18% swing, then swap kit pieces and edit accents in the piano roll.
Routing
Route drums to a General MIDI Drum Rack or kit, keep bass mono and separate from chord stabs, and use returns for delay/reverb so loop edits stay fast.
Effects
Ableton stock starting chain: EQ Eight high-pass on chords, Auto Filter for movement, Glue Compressor on the music bus, and short Delay/Reverb sends.
Ableton bridge setup
Ableton bridge profile: stock-device setup with layer-specific volume balance and simple tone controls. Use saved jamburgr racks later if you want a more personal sound while keeping the same MIDI.
Listen for
Listen for how short chord stabs, offbeat bass, swung percussion, and small mutes make a loop feel alive without constant new material. Also compare the generated groove feel against: Four-on-the-floor pulse with swung percussion, offbeat emphasis, and loop-friendly chord movement.

house / 124 BPM / minimal_deep_tech

Minimal deep tech

Minimal deep tech draws on minimal house, Romanian minimal, and tech-house restraint for long-form groove work.

AKA
minimal deep tech, deep tech, minimal house
Geography
Chicago, New York, London, Paris, Ibiza, South Africa, and global club circuits.
Era
2000s-present
Groove feel
Four-on-the-floor pulse with swung percussion, offbeat emphasis, and loop-friendly chord movement.
Harmonic habits
Short modal cells, seventh chords, add9 colors, and progressions that leave room for drums and bass.

Layer defaults

Scale
natural_minor
Voicing
closed
Pattern
offbeat_stabs
Bass
offbeat_house @ octave 1
Pad
fifth_drone @ octave 4
Lead
simple_motif @ octave 5
Lead feel
sparse / high
Drum style
house_shuffle
Drum density
sparse
Drum swing
14%

Drum role

House shuffle — A swung club scaffold with kick/clap weight and loose hat or shaker motion.

Use a warm Drum Rack, 909-style kit, or sampled house kit and keep the hats editable for groove feel.

Density sparse. Sparse sketches the pocket; medium adds shuffled hats; dense adds extra top-loop energy. Swing hint: 14%. Drum export is General MIDI only; enable it with generate_drums: true.

Producer setup recipe

Use this as a practical Ableton-friendly starting point, then choose your own sounds and edit the MIDI for the track you are making.

Chords
Ableton Analog/Drift for short filtered stabs, or Prophet-10-style poly stabs with a fast amp envelope
Bass
Ableton Drift or Analog mono bass with short decay, centered low end, and enough filter movement to answer the kick
Pad
Ableton Wavetable or Analog drone with slow attack, low resonance, and subtle movement
Lead
Ableton Operator, Drift, or Wavetable for a simple motif or chord-tone lead above the harmony
Drums
Use the generated General MIDI drum lane with an Ableton Drum Rack, GM kit, or hardware drum route. Start from `house_shuffle` at `sparse` density with 14% swing, then swap kit pieces and edit accents in the piano roll.
Routing
Route drums to a General MIDI Drum Rack or kit, keep bass mono and separate from chord stabs, and use returns for delay/reverb so loop edits stay fast.
Effects
Ableton stock starting chain: EQ Eight high-pass on chords, Auto Filter for movement, Glue Compressor on the music bus, and short Delay/Reverb sends.
Ableton bridge setup
Ableton bridge-ready direction: start with stock synth or rack choices, then map stable macros such as Tone, Movement, Brightness, Drive, Width, FX, Attack, and Release for fast style-aware setup.
Listen for
Listen for how short chord stabs, offbeat bass, swung percussion, and small mutes make a loop feel alive without constant new material. Also compare the generated groove feel against: Four-on-the-floor pulse with swung percussion, offbeat emphasis, and loop-friendly chord movement.

Hardware

  • Create an original offbeat chord stab layer, then duplicate it an octave up for a lighter variation.
  • Use pack mode to compare chord, bass, and pad lanes as separate DAW clips.

Producer setup recipe

Use this as a practical Ableton-friendly starting point, then choose your own sounds and edit the MIDI for the track you are making.

Chords
Ableton Analog/Drift for short filtered stabs, or Prophet-10-style poly stabs with a fast amp envelope
Bass
Ableton Drift, Analog, or Operator for a clean mono bass that follows the generated root motion
Pad
Ableton Wavetable, Meld, or Analog for a sustained pad layer that can be muted or widened independently
Lead
Ableton Operator, Drift, or Wavetable for a simple motif or chord-tone lead above the harmony
Drums
Use the generated General MIDI drum lane with an Ableton Drum Rack, GM kit, or hardware drum route. Start from `percussion_pulse` at `sparse` density with 14% swing, then swap kit pieces and edit accents in the piano roll.
Routing
Route drums to a General MIDI Drum Rack or kit, keep bass mono and separate from chord stabs, and use returns for delay/reverb so loop edits stay fast.
Effects
Ableton stock starting chain: EQ Eight high-pass on chords, Auto Filter for movement, Glue Compressor on the music bus, and short Delay/Reverb sends.
Ableton bridge setup
Ableton bridge-ready direction: start with stock synth or rack choices, then map stable macros such as Tone, Movement, Brightness, Drive, Width, FX, Attack, and Release for fast style-aware setup.
Listen for
Listen for how short chord stabs, offbeat bass, swung percussion, and small mutes make a loop feel alive without constant new material. Also compare the generated groove feel against: Four-on-the-floor pulse with swung percussion, offbeat emphasis, and loop-friendly chord movement.

Drum role

Garage skip — Syncopated 2-step-style placement for garage, bassline, and swung house sketches.

Use a crisp kit with short hats and claps, then nudge or quantize selectively inside the DAW.

Density medium. Sparse preserves the skip; medium adds hat answers; dense adds shaker texture and extra kicks. Swing hint: 30%. Drum export is General MIDI only; enable it with generate_drums: true.

Producer setup recipe

Use this as a practical Ableton-friendly starting point, then choose your own sounds and edit the MIDI for the track you are making.

Chords
Ableton Analog/Drift for short filtered stabs, or Prophet-10-style poly stabs with a fast amp envelope
Bass
Ableton Drift, Analog, or Operator for a clean mono bass that follows the generated root motion
Pad
Ableton Wavetable, Meld, or Analog for a sustained pad layer that can be muted or widened independently
Lead
Ableton Operator, Drift, or Wavetable for a simple motif or chord-tone lead above the harmony
Drums
Use the generated General MIDI drum lane with an Ableton Drum Rack, GM kit, or hardware drum route. Start from `garage_skip` at `medium` density with 30% swing, then swap kit pieces and edit accents in the piano roll.
Routing
Keep drums and bass editable as their own lanes. Route breaks or GM drums to a kit, center sub movement, and let chord chops sit above the low end.
Effects
Ableton stock starting chain: EQ Eight on breaks and bass, Drum Buss for transient weight, Auto Filter on stabs, and short room/plate sends.
Ableton bridge setup
Ableton bridge-ready direction: keep each generated layer on its own track, use stock devices or personal racks, and save any favorite setup as a jamburgr rack with stable macros.
Listen for
Listen for the push-pull between break or garage timing, bass answers, and compact chord punctuation. Also compare the generated groove feel against: Breakbeat or swung garage timing, strong bass answers, and syncopated chord placement.

Half-time — Wide snare spacing and downbeat weight for bass music, dubstep, and wave/hardwave.

Producer setup recipe

Use this as a practical Ableton-friendly starting point, then choose your own sounds and edit the MIDI for the track you are making.

Chords

Ableton Wavetable/Drift short pluck or chopped sampler layer with MIDI kept original and editable
Drums
Use the generated General MIDI drum lane with an Ableton Drum Rack, GM kit, or hardware drum route. Start from `half_time` at `medium` density with 0% swing, then swap kit pieces and edit accents in the piano roll.
Routing
Keep drums and bass editable as their own lanes. Route breaks or GM drums to a kit, center sub movement, and let chord chops sit above the low end.
Effects
Ableton stock starting chain: EQ Eight on breaks and bass, Drum Buss for transient weight, Auto Filter on stabs, and short room/plate sends.
Ableton bridge setup
Ableton bridge-ready direction: keep each generated layer on its own track, use stock devices or personal racks, and save any favorite setup as a jamburgr rack with stable macros.
Listen for
Listen for the push-pull between break or garage timing, bass answers, and compact chord punctuation. Also compare the generated groove feel against: Breakbeat or swung garage timing, strong bass answers, and syncopated chord placement.
Chords

short filtered chord stab instrument

Clear harmonic color that supports the groove without covering bass, lead, or drums.

Mix role
Midrange harmonic identity; high-pass and balance below the lead but above bass fundamentals.
Effects/routing
Start with EQ cleanup, filter movement, and shared delay/reverb sends rather than printing effects into the MIDI idea.
Hardware
Prophet-10-style poly patches are a strong hardware option for warm chords, stabs, and pads.
Tags
stock_ableton, saved_rack_ready, hardware_poly

wide Reese or detuned bass synth with mono low end

Detuned motion and low-end pressure with the sub content kept centered.

Mix role
Centered low-end anchor; keep it mono-friendly and leave headroom for drums.
Effects/routing
Use EQ and light saturation; avoid wide modulation below the sub range and add sidechain or volume shaping only after the groove works.
Hardware
Moog Matriarch-style mono patches work well for bass, acid-style lines, resonant plucks, and hardware takes.

bass music / 150 BPM / trap_edm

EDM trap / future trap

EDM trap translates Southern hip-hop drum language and bass-music drops into electronic festival arrangements.

AKA
EDM trap, future trap, festival trap
Geography
UK and North American bass scenes, online producer communities, and festival bass stages.
Era
2010s-present
Groove feel
Half-time or syncopated drums with strong downbeat weight, spacious snare placement, and sub-focused movement.
Harmonic habits
Minor-mode loops, suspended color tones, add9 sonorities, and dramatic tension between bass roots and bright upper stacks.

Drum role

Trap hat — 808/trap-informed hat motion with sparse kick and snare placement.

Use Drum Rack, a GM kit, or an 808-style sampler and edit hat rolls after import.

Density dense. Sparse is minimal; medium adds steady hats; dense adds faster hat subdivisions. Swing hint: 0%. Drum export is General MIDI only; enable it with generate_drums: true.

Producer setup recipe

Use this as a practical Ableton-friendly starting point, then choose your own sounds and edit the MIDI for the track you are making.

Chords
Ableton Wavetable or Analog for poly chords, with a hardware-friendly subtractive poly patch as an alternative
Bass
Ableton Simpler/Sampler or Drift sine-sub patch with glide, tuned to the key and kept clean below the chord stack
Pad
Ableton Wavetable or Analog drone with slow attack, low resonance, and subtle movement
Lead
Ableton Operator, Drift, or Wavetable for a simple motif or chord-tone lead above the harmony
Drums
Use the generated General MIDI drum lane with an Ableton Drum Rack, GM kit, or hardware drum route. Start from `trap_hat` at `dense` density with 0% swing, then swap kit pieces and edit accents in the piano roll.
Routing
Keep bass, drums, chords, pads, and lead on separate MIDI tracks. Center the sub layer, leave headroom for kick/snare weight, and use sidechain or volume shaping only after the MIDI idea is working.
Effects
Ableton stock starting chain: EQ Eight cleanup, Saturator for controlled edge, Compressor or sidechain ducking, and Echo/Reverb sends for impacts.
Ableton bridge setup
Ableton bridge-ready direction: keep each generated layer on its own track, use stock devices or personal racks, and save any favorite setup as a jamburgr rack with stable macros.
Listen for
Listen for the relationship between sub movement, snare placement, wide harmony, and moments where the arrangement gets smaller before it gets larger. Also compare the generated groove feel against: Half-time or syncopated drums with strong downbeat weight, spacious snare placement, and sub-focused movement.

Listen for the push-pull between break or garage timing, bass answers, and compact chord punctuation. Also compare the generated groove feel against: Breakbeat or swung garage timing, strong bass answers, and syncopated chord placement.
Chords

short filtered chord stab instrument

Clear harmonic color that supports the groove without covering bass, lead, or drums.

Mix role
Midrange harmonic identity; high-pass and balance below the lead but above bass fundamentals.
Effects/routing

Hardware
Prophet-10-style poly patches are a strong hardware option for warm chords, stabs, and pads.

dnb_atmospheric @ octave 6

Drum role

DnB two-step — Fast two-step kick/snare orientation for drum and bass and liquid lanes.

Route to a break kit or Drum Rack, then layer snares and edit ghost hits around the bass.

Density medium. Sparse marks the backbeat; medium adds hats; dense adds faster hat and ghost-note movement. Swing hint: 4%. Drum export is General MIDI only; enable it with generate_drums: true.

Producer setup recipe

Use this as a practical Ableton-friendly starting point, then choose your own sounds and edit the MIDI for the track you are making.

Chords
Ableton Analog/Drift for short filtered stabs, or Prophet-10-style poly stabs with a fast amp envelope
Bass
Ableton Drift, Analog, or Operator for a clean mono bass that follows the generated root motion
Pad
Ableton Wavetable, Meld, or Analog for a sustained pad layer that can be muted or widened independently
Lead
Ableton Operator bell, Wavetable air layer, or a resampled one-shot placed above pads
Drums
Use the generated General MIDI drum lane with an Ableton Drum Rack, GM kit, or hardware drum route. Start from `dnb_two_step` at `medium` density with 4% swing, then swap kit pieces and edit accents in the piano roll.
Routing
Keep drums and bass editable as their own lanes. Route breaks or GM drums to a kit, center sub movement, and let chord chops sit above the low end.
Effects
Ableton stock starting chain: EQ Eight on breaks and bass, Drum Buss for transient weight, Auto Filter on stabs, and short room/plate sends.
Ableton bridge setup
Ableton bridge-ready direction: keep each generated layer on its own track, use stock devices or personal racks, and save any favorite setup as a jamburgr rack with stable macros.
Listen for
Listen for the push-pull between break or garage timing, bass answers, and compact chord punctuation. Also compare the generated groove feel against: Breakbeat or swung garage timing, strong bass answers, and syncopated chord placement.

Density medium. Sparse keeps the machine groove clean; medium adds accent voices; dense adds sixteenth drive. Swing hint: 0%. Drum export is General MIDI only; enable it with generate_drums: true.

Producer setup recipe

Use this as a practical Ableton-friendly starting point, then choose your own sounds and edit the MIDI for the track you are making.

Effects

Ableton bridge setup

electro syncopated drum scaffold at medium density with 0% swing for DAW editing.

Hardware

Tags
stock_ableton, saved_rack_ready, general_midi, drum_rack
analog-style bassgated supersawsFM bellsrave stabssequenced arps

Gear and synthesis

Roland TR-909 lineage, Roland TB-303 lineage, step sequencers, analog monosynths

resonant filter sweeps, tempo-synced gates, acid slides, supersaw detune, FM plucks

Listen for

long builds, filter-open tension, drum-led breakdowns, return-to-groove drops

tempo delay, large hall reverb, drive saturation, sidechain compression

Try this in your DAW

  • Limit the harmony to one or two Roman numerals and make motion through inversion, register, and pattern.
  • Render a pack, then mute lanes one by one to find the smallest loop that still carries the style.
  • Write a sixteen-bar section where the chord MIDI stays stable but lead density rises gradually.

techno and trance / 150 BPM / hardstyle

Hardstyle / euphoric hard dance

Hardstyle developed from hard trance, hardcore, and Dutch/European hard dance scenes with a signature kick-led structure.

AKA
hardstyle, euphoric hardstyle, hard dance
Geography
Detroit, Berlin, Frankfurt, Goa, the Netherlands, and international warehouse/festival scenes.
Era
2000s-present
Groove feel
Motorik repetition, steady kick pressure, gated arps, and hypnotic phrase evolution.
Harmonic habits
Modal minor movement, pedal tones, chromatic tension, and long arcs built from small cells.

Layer defaults

Scale
natural_minor
Voicing
open
Pattern
trance_gate
Bass
octave_pulse @ octave 1
Pad
high_shimmer @ octave 5
Lead
trance_pluck @ octave 5
Lead feel
dense / high
Drum style
four_on_floor
Drum density
dense
Drum swing
0%

Drum role

Four-on-the-floor — Steady kick pulse for house, trance, synthwave, and other grid-forward ideas.

Drop the lane onto a General MIDI kit or Drum Rack, then choose a kick, clap, and hat palette that fits the track.

Density dense. Sparse keeps kick/clap shape; medium adds offbeat hats; dense adds busier hats and lift. Swing hint: 0%. Drum export is General MIDI only; enable it with generate_drums: true.

Producer setup recipe

Use this as a practical Ableton-friendly starting point, then choose your own sounds and edit the MIDI for the track you are making.

Chords
Ableton Wavetable/Analog for gated chords or rave stabs, with a hardware poly option for wide sustained layers
Bass
Ableton Drift, Analog, or Operator for a clean mono bass that follows the generated root motion
Pad
Ableton Wavetable, Meld, or Analog for a sustained pad layer that can be muted or widened independently
Lead
Ableton Operator or Wavetable pluck with tempo delay, or a Matriarch-style resonant mono pluck for hardware takes
Drums
Use the generated General MIDI drum lane with an Ableton Drum Rack, GM kit, or hardware drum route. Start from `four_on_floor` at `dense` density with 0% swing, then swap kit pieces and edit accents in the piano roll.
Routing
Use separate tracks for pulse, drones, arps, and drums. Keep the kick/bass lane focused, then automate filters or mutes across sections instead of overfilling the MIDI.
Effects
Ableton stock starting chain: Auto Filter automation, Saturator or Roar for drive if available, Echo on arps, and large reverb sends for breakdown space.
Ableton bridge setup
Ableton bridge-ready direction: start with stock synth or rack choices, then map stable macros such as Tone, Movement, Brightness, Drive, Width, FX, Attack, and Release for fast style-aware setup.
Listen for
Listen for gradual filter motion, pedal tones, gated or arpeggiated repetition, and long tension curves across sections. Also compare the generated groove feel against: Motorik repetition, steady kick pressure, gated arps, and hypnotic phrase evolution.
Chords

polyphonic chord synth

Clear harmonic color that supports the groove without covering bass, lead, or drums.

Mix role
Midrange harmonic identity; high-pass and balance below the lead but above bass fundamentals.
Effects/routing
Start with EQ cleanup, filter movement, and shared delay/reverb sends rather than printing effects into the MIDI idea.
Hardware
Prophet-10-style poly patches are a strong hardware option for warm chords, stabs, and pads.
Tags
stock_ableton, saved_rack_ready, hardware_poly, commercial_core_synth_optional

clean mono bass synth

Centered low-end motion that makes the generated roots feel intentional and editable.

Mix role
Centered low-end anchor; keep it mono-friendly and leave headroom for drums.
Effects/routing
Use EQ and light saturation; avoid wide modulation below the sub range and add sidechain or volume shaping only after the groove works.
Hardware
Moog Matriarch-style mono patches work well for bass, acid-style lines, resonant plucks, and hardware takes.

Use the generated General MIDI drum lane with an Ableton Drum Rack, GM kit, or hardware drum route. Start from `four_on_floor` at `medium` density with 0% swing, then swap kit pieces and edit accents in the piano roll.
Routing
Use wide pads/chords, a centered bass track, and a soft drum or percussion lane. Keep delay/reverb on returns so the sketch stays easy to rebalance.
Effects
Ableton stock starting chain: Chorus-Ensemble or subtle modulation, EQ Eight, Echo, Hybrid Reverb/Reverb sends, and gentle bus compression.
Ableton bridge setup
Ableton bridge profile: Wavetable chords/pad/lead, Drift bass, and 909 Core Kit drums, with conservative volumes and editable stock parameter defaults for a more listenable first sketch.
Listen for
Listen for pad width, simple bass movement, nostalgic timbre, and the way reverb/delay length changes emotional scale. Also compare the generated groove feel against: Relaxed tempos, steady arps, soft syncopation, and nostalgia-forward chord sustain.

Transient and groove reference; route to an editable drum instrument and balance before adding heavy processing.
Effects/routing
Use Drum Rack or a GM-compatible kit first, then swap sounds, tune hits, and add Drum Buss or saturation to taste.
Hardware
External drum machines or sampler kits can follow the General MIDI lane after note mapping is checked.
Tags
stock_ableton, saved_rack_ready, general_midi, drum_rack
analog-style polysynthsJuno-style padsFM bellsdrum machinestape-warmed keys

Gear and synthesis

Roland Juno lineage, Yamaha DX lineage, Roland TR-808 lineage, cassette or tape processors

chorused pads, slow filter envelopes, soft detune, noise layers, tape-style modulation

Listen for

long intros, melodic toplines, nostalgic breakdowns, slow pad reveals

chorus, ensemble, tape delay, plate reverb, gentle saturation

Try this in your DAW

  • Lock the topline across a four-chord loop and compare it with open voicing for emotional contour.
  • Generate a pad lane and a lead lane, then thin the arrangement until the main mood still reads.
  • Use velocity and humanize settings to make a rigid MIDI loop feel less grid-bound.

experimental / 118 BPM / idm_glitch

IDM / glitch electronic

IDM and glitch electronic music developed through experimental listening scenes, software tools, and leftfield club-adjacent practice.

AKA
IDM, glitch electronic, experimental electronica
Geography
UK, North American, European, and online experimental electronic communities.
Era
1990s-present
Groove feel
Asymmetry, broken grids, Euclidean accents, and tension between machine precision and humanized offsets.
Harmonic habits
Chromatic cells, clusters, quartal shapes, pedal tones, and unstable modal centers.

Layer defaults

Scale
chromatic
Voicing
cluster
Pattern
euclidean
Bass
pedal_tone @ octave 1
Pad
cluster @ octave 4
Lead
arp_random @ octave 5
Lead feel
dense / low
Drum style
percussion_pulse
Drum density
medium
Drum swing
10%

Drum role

Percussion pulse — Clave, tom, shaker, and rim scaffolding for organic, global-club, and experimental lanes.

Map to hand percussion, synthetic drums, or a GM kit, then swap voices to match your session.

Density medium. Sparse leaves space for bass and vocals; medium adds pulse; dense adds more hand-percussion motion. Swing hint: 10%. Drum export is General MIDI only; enable it with generate_drums: true.

Producer setup recipe

Use this as a practical Ableton-friendly starting point, then choose your own sounds and edit the MIDI for the track you are making.

Chords
Ableton Wavetable or Meld with restrained voices, or a hardware poly synth with close voicing and light modulation
Bass
Ableton Drift, Analog, or Operator for a clean mono bass that follows the generated root motion
Pad
Ableton Meld/Wavetable for controlled dissonant texture, filtered so clusters support rather than crowd the track
Lead
Ableton Operator, Drift, or Wavetable for a simple motif or chord-tone lead above the harmony
Drums
Use the generated General MIDI drum lane with an Ableton Drum Rack, GM kit, or hardware drum route. Start from `percussion_pulse` at `medium` density with 10% swing, then swap kit pieces and edit accents in the piano roll.
Routing
Keep every layer isolated for muting, resampling, and rearranging. Treat the MIDI as a structured sketch that can feed stock synths, samplers, or hardware routes.
Effects
Ableton stock starting chain: Auto Filter, Beat Repeat or Grain Delay-style edits where appropriate, Utility for width control, and restrained sends.
Ableton bridge setup
Ableton bridge-ready direction: keep each generated layer on its own track, use stock devices or personal racks, and save any favorite setup as a jamburgr rack with stable macros.
Listen for
Listen for texture, negative space, asymmetry, and the way a small MIDI cell can become a sound-design system. Also compare the generated groove feel against: Asymmetry, broken grids, Euclidean accents, and tension between machine precision and humanized offsets.
Chords

textural poly synth or controlled dissonance rack

Controlled tension and close intervals, filtered so the color stays musical rather than harsh.

Mix role
Midrange harmonic identity; high-pass and balance below the lead but above bass fundamentals.
Effects/routing
Start with EQ cleanup, filter movement, and shared delay/reverb sends rather than printing effects into the MIDI idea.
Hardware
Prophet-10-style poly patches are a strong hardware option for warm chords, stabs, and pads.
Tags
stock_ableton, saved_rack_ready, hardware_poly

Gear and synthesis

Listen for

bitcrushing, comb filtering, spectral delay, distortion sends, wide modulation

Try this in your DAW

  • Start with a legal scale, then use cluster voicing and sparse lead density to add controlled instability.
  • Render multiple variations and choose the one with the most useful accidents for DAW editing.
  • Separate bass and pad lanes so low-end pressure remains usable even when upper harmony gets abstract.

house / 118 BPM / lofi_house

Lo-fi house

Lo-fi house became prominent through online scenes and underground house communities favoring rough edges and nostalgic samples.

AKA
lo-fi house, outsider house, dusty house
Geography
Chicago, New York, London, Paris, Ibiza, South Africa, and global club circuits.
Era
2010s-present
Groove feel
Four-on-the-floor pulse with swung percussion, offbeat emphasis, and loop-friendly chord movement.
Harmonic habits
Short modal cells, seventh chords, add9 colors, and progressions that leave room for drums and bass.

Layer defaults

Scale
natural_minor
Voicing
drop2
Pattern
garage_chops
Bass
offbeat_house @ octave 1
Pad
slow_wide @ octave 4
Lead
chord_tone_lead @ octave 5
Lead feel
sparse / high
Drum style
house_shuffle
Drum density
sparse
Drum swing
24%

Drum role

House shuffle — A swung club scaffold with kick/clap weight and loose hat or shaker motion.

Use a warm Drum Rack, 909-style kit, or sampled house kit and keep the hats editable for groove feel.

Density sparse. Sparse sketches the pocket; medium adds shuffled hats; dense adds extra top-loop energy. Swing hint: 24%. Drum export is General MIDI only; enable it with generate_drums: true.

Producer setup recipe

Use this as a practical Ableton-friendly starting point, then choose your own sounds and edit the MIDI for the track you are making.

Chords
Ableton Analog/Drift for short filtered stabs, or Prophet-10-style poly stabs with a fast amp envelope
Bass
Ableton Drift or Analog mono bass with short decay, centered low end, and enough filter movement to answer the kick
Pad
Ableton Wavetable, Meld, or Analog for a sustained pad layer that can be muted or widened independently
Lead
Ableton Operator, Drift, or Wavetable for a simple motif or chord-tone lead above the harmony
Drums
Use the generated General MIDI drum lane with an Ableton Drum Rack, GM kit, or hardware drum route. Start from `house_shuffle` at `sparse` density with 24% swing, then swap kit pieces and edit accents in the piano roll.
Routing
Route drums to a General MIDI Drum Rack or kit, keep bass mono and separate from chord stabs, and use returns for delay/reverb so loop edits stay fast.
Effects
Ableton stock starting chain: EQ Eight high-pass on chords, Auto Filter for movement, Glue Compressor on the music bus, and short Delay/Reverb sends.
Ableton bridge setup
Ableton bridge-ready direction: start with stock synth or rack choices, then map stable macros such as Tone, Movement, Brightness, Drive, Width, FX, Attack, and Release for fast style-aware setup.
Listen for
Listen for how short chord stabs, offbeat bass, swung percussion, and small mutes make a loop feel alive without constant new material. Also compare the generated groove feel against: Four-on-the-floor pulse with swung percussion, offbeat emphasis, and loop-friendly chord movement.
Chords

short filtered chord stab instrument

Rhythmic garage chops chords with enough transient edge to read as a groove part.

Mix role
Midrange harmonic identity; high-pass and balance below the lead but above bass fundamentals.
Effects/routing
Start with EQ cleanup, filter movement, and shared delay/reverb sends rather than printing effects into the MIDI idea.
Hardware
Prophet-10-style poly patches are a strong hardware option for warm chords, stabs, and pads.
Tags
stock_ableton, saved_rack_ready, hardware_poly

electric pianoorgan stabssampled chord chopssub bassdrum machine percussion

Gear and synthesis

Roland TR-909 lineage, Roland TR-808 lineage, Akai-style samplers, MIDI chord modules

filter envelopes, sample filtering, short amp envelopes, chorused keys, subtractive bass patches

Listen for

DJ-friendly intros, incremental mutes, breakdowns, drop returns, loop variation

bus compression, delay sends, filtered transitions, spring or plate reverb

Try this in your DAW

  • Make a two-chord groove and change only rhythm, voicing, and bass placement over sixteen bars.
  • Create an original offbeat chord stab layer, then duplicate it an octave up for a lighter variation.
  • Use pack mode to compare chord, bass, and pad lanes as separate DAW clips.

Recipe Config Library

Original recipes and study configs for every style.

The library is moving from broad study configs toward named Jam Library recipes. Authored recipe sets are available for: Uplifting trance, Deep house, Tech house, French house / disco house, Afro house / organic groove, UK garage / 2-step chords, Amapiano / log-drum inspired, Synthwave / outrun. Amapiano native log-drum and percussion behavior is still tracked as product work. Remaining styles still expose the original study configs until their recipe sets land.

run a recipe config
python jamburgr.py --config configs/recipes/synthwave/synthwave_night_drive_arp.md

bass music

Future bass / wonky emotional

future_bass

Ten original study configs for this style, with chords, bass, pads, leads, and editable General MIDI drums enabled. Run any file with python jamburgr.py --config configs/recipes/future_bass/filename.md.

  1. arp motion study configs/recipes/future_bass/future_bass_arp_motion_study.md Atlas
  2. chop and stab study configs/recipes/future_bass/future_bass_chop_and_stab_study.md Atlas
